\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00199}00199   \textcolor{comment}{// Data latch = 300+ microsecond pause in the output stream. Rather than}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00200}00200   \textcolor{comment}{// put a delay at the end of the function, the ending time is noted and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00201}00201   \textcolor{comment}{// the function will simply hold off (if needed) on issuing the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00202}00202   \textcolor{comment}{// subsequent round of data until the latch time has elapsed. This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00203}00203   \textcolor{comment}{// allows the mainline code to start generating the next frame of data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00204}00204   \textcolor{comment}{// rather than stalling for the latch.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00205}00205   \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(!\mbox{\hyperlink{class_adafruit___neo_pixel_a9e900a60b0ac2b43b99309bb118b929e}{canShow}}());}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00206}00206   \textcolor{comment}{// endTime is a private member (rather than global var) so that multiple}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00207}00207   \textcolor{comment}{// instances on different pins can be quickly issued in succession (each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00208}00208   \textcolor{comment}{// instance doesn't delay the next).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00209}00209 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00210}00210   \textcolor{comment}{// In order to make this code runtime-\/configurable to work with any pin,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00211}00211   \textcolor{comment}{// SBI/CBI instructions are eschewed in favor of full PORT writes via the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00212}00212   \textcolor{comment}{// OUT or ST instructions. It relies on two facts: that peripheral}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00213}00213   \textcolor{comment}{// functions (such as PWM) take precedence on output pins, so our PORT-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00214}00214   \textcolor{comment}{// wide writes won't interfere, and that interrupts are globally disabled}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00215}00215   \textcolor{comment}{// while data is being issued to the LEDs, so no other code will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00216}00216   \textcolor{comment}{// accessing the PORT. The code takes an initial 'snapshot' of the PORT}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00217}00217   \textcolor{comment}{// state, computes 'pin high' and 'pin low' values, and writes these back}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00218}00218   \textcolor{comment}{// to the PORT register as needed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l00219}00219 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01338}01338 \textcolor{comment}{// [[[Begin of the Neopixel NRF52 EasyDMA implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01339}01339 \textcolor{comment}{//                                    by the Hackerspace San Salvador]]]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01340}01340 \textcolor{comment}{// This technique uses the PWM peripheral on the NRF52. The PWM uses the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01341}01341 \textcolor{comment}{// EasyDMA feature included on the chip. This technique loads the duty}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01342}01342 \textcolor{comment}{// cycle configuration for each cycle when the PWM is enabled. For this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01343}01343 \textcolor{comment}{// to work we need to store a 16 bit configuration for each bit of the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01344}01344 \textcolor{comment}{// RGB(W) values in the pixel buffer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01345}01345 \textcolor{comment}{// Comparator values for the PWM were hand picked and are guaranteed to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01346}01346 \textcolor{comment}{// be 100\% organic to preserve freshness and high accuracy. Current}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01347}01347 \textcolor{comment}{// parameters are:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01348}01348 \textcolor{comment}{//   * PWM Clock: 16Mhz}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01349}01349 \textcolor{comment}{//   * Minimum step time: 62.5ns}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01350}01350 \textcolor{comment}{//   * Time for zero in high (T0H): 0.31ms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01351}01351 \textcolor{comment}{//   * Time for one in high (T1H): 0.75ms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01352}01352 \textcolor{comment}{//   * Cycle time:  1.25us}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01353}01353 \textcolor{comment}{//   * Frequency: 800Khz}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01354}01354 \textcolor{comment}{// For 400Khz we just double the calculated times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01355}01355 \textcolor{comment}{// -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/ BEGIN Constants for the EasyDMA implementation -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01356}01356 \textcolor{comment}{// The PWM starts the duty cycle in LOW. To start with HIGH we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01357}01357 \textcolor{comment}{// need to set the 15th bit on each register.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01358}01358 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01394}01394   \textcolor{comment}{// To support both the SoftDevice + Neopixels we use the EasyDMA}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01395}01395   \textcolor{comment}{// feature from the NRF25. However this technique implies to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01396}01396   \textcolor{comment}{// generate a pattern and store it on the memory. The actual}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01724}01724   \textcolor{comment}{// SAMD51 overclock-\/compatible timing is only a mild abomination.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01725}01725   \textcolor{comment}{// It uses SysTick for a consistent clock reference regardless of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01726}01726   \textcolor{comment}{// optimization / cache settings.  That's the good news.  The bad news,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01727}01727   \textcolor{comment}{// since SysTick-\/>VAL is a volatile type it's slow to access...and then,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01728}01728   \textcolor{comment}{// with the SysTick interval that Arduino sets up (1 ms), this would}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01729}01729   \textcolor{comment}{// require a subtract and MOD operation for gauging elapsed time, and}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01730}01730   \textcolor{comment}{// all taken in combination that lacks adequate temporal resolution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01731}01731   \textcolor{comment}{// for NeoPixel timing.  So a kind of horrible thing is done here...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01732}01732   \textcolor{comment}{// since interrupts are turned off anyway and it's generally accepted}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01733}01733   \textcolor{comment}{// by now that we're gonna lose track of time in the NeoPixel lib,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01734}01734   \textcolor{comment}{// the SysTick timer is reconfigured for a period matching the NeoPixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01735}01735   \textcolor{comment}{// bit timing (either 800 or 400 KHz) and we watch SysTick-\/>VAL very}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01736}01736   \textcolor{comment}{// closely (just a threshold, no subtract or MOD or anything) and that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01737}01737   \textcolor{comment}{// seems to work just well enough.  When finished, the SysTick}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l01738}01738   \textcolor{comment}{// peripheral is set back to its original state.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02125}02125   \textcolor{comment}{// Because of the caching process, "{}CPU slows down"{}. NEOPIXEL pulse is very time sensitive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02126}02126   \textcolor{comment}{// that's why we let the CPU cache first and we start regular pulse from 2nd iteration}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02386}02386 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02387}02387   uint8\_t r, g, b;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02388}02388 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02389}02389   \textcolor{comment}{// Remap 0-\/65535 to 0-\/1529. Pure red is CENTERED on the 64K rollover;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02390}02390   \textcolor{comment}{// 0 is not the start of pure red, but the midpoint...a few values above}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02391}02391   \textcolor{comment}{// zero and a few below 65536 all yield pure red (similarly, 32768 is the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02392}02392   \textcolor{comment}{// midpoint, not start, of pure cyan). The 8-\/bit RGB hexcone (256 values}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02393}02393   \textcolor{comment}{// each for red, green, blue) really only allows for 1530 distinct hues}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02394}02394   \textcolor{comment}{// (not 1536, more on that below), but the full unsigned 16-\/bit type was}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02395}02395   \textcolor{comment}{// chosen for hue so that one's code can easily handle a contiguous color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02396}02396   \textcolor{comment}{// wheel by allowing hue to roll over in either direction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02397}02397   hue = (hue * 1530L + 32768) / 65536;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02398}02398   \textcolor{comment}{// Because red is centered on the rollover point (the +32768 above,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02399}02399   \textcolor{comment}{// essentially a fixed-\/point +0.5), the above actually yields 0 to 1530,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02400}02400   \textcolor{comment}{// where 0 and 1530 would yield the same thing. Rather than apply a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02401}02401   \textcolor{comment}{// costly modulo operator, 1530 is handled as a special case below.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02402}02402 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02403}02403   \textcolor{comment}{// So you'd think that the color "{}hexcone"{} (the thing that ramps from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02404}02404   \textcolor{comment}{// pure red, to pure yellow, to pure green and so forth back to red,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02405}02405   \textcolor{comment}{// yielding six slices), and with each color component having 256}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02406}02406   \textcolor{comment}{// possible values (0-\/255), might have 1536 possible items (6*256),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02407}02407   \textcolor{comment}{// but in reality there's 1530. This is because the last element in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02408}02408   \textcolor{comment}{// each 256-\/element slice is equal to the first element of the next}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02409}02409   \textcolor{comment}{// slice, and keeping those in there this would create small}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02410}02410   \textcolor{comment}{// discontinuities in the color wheel. So the last element of each}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02411}02411   \textcolor{comment}{// slice is dropped...we regard only elements 0-\/254, with item 255}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02412}02412   \textcolor{comment}{// being picked up as element 0 of the next slice. Like this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02413}02413   \textcolor{comment}{// Red to not-\/quite-\/pure-\/yellow is:        255,   0, 0 to 255, 254,   0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02414}02414   \textcolor{comment}{// Pure yellow to not-\/quite-\/pure-\/green is: 255, 255, 0 to   1, 255,   0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02415}02415   \textcolor{comment}{// Pure green to not-\/quite-\/pure-\/cyan is:     0, 255, 0 to   0, 255, 254}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02416}02416   \textcolor{comment}{// and so forth. Hence, 1530 distinct hues (0 to 1529), and hence why}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02417}02417   \textcolor{comment}{// the constants below are not the multiples of 256 you might expect.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02418}02418 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02419}02419   \textcolor{comment}{// Convert hue to R,G,B (nested ifs faster than divide+mod+switch):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02420}02420   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(hue < 510) \{         \textcolor{comment}{// Red to Green-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02421}02421     b = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02422}02422     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(hue < 255) \{       \textcolor{comment}{//   Red to Yellow-\/1}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02424}02424       g = hue;            \textcolor{comment}{//     g = 0 to 254}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02452}02452   \textcolor{comment}{// Apply saturation and value to R,G,B, pack into 32-\/bit result:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02536}02536     \textcolor{comment}{// This process is potentially "{}lossy,"{} especially when increasing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02537}02537     \textcolor{comment}{// brightness. The tight timing in the WS2811/WS2812 code means there}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02538}02538     \textcolor{comment}{// aren't enough free cycles to perform this scaling on the fly as data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02539}02539     \textcolor{comment}{// is issued. So we make a pass through the existing color data in RAM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02540}02540     \textcolor{comment}{// and scale it (subsequent graphics commands also work at this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02541}02541     \textcolor{comment}{// brightness level). If there's a significant step up in brightness,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02542}02542     \textcolor{comment}{// the limited number of steps (quantization) in the old data will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02543}02543     \textcolor{comment}{// quite visible in the re-\/scaled version. For a non-\/destructive}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_adafruit___neo_pixel_8cpp_source_l02544}02544     \textcolor{comment}{// change, you'll need to re-\/render the full strip data. C'est la vie.}}
